## Summaries
### Difference between the two
#### Tenets

|                   | Classical                                                                                                                 | Modern                                                                                                                                      |
| ----------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Individualism     | Egoistical individualism                                                                                                  | Developmental individualism                                                                                                                 |
| Freedom           | Negative freedom                                                                                                          | Positive freedom                                                                                                                            |
| State             | > Fears the state acting in society<br>> Welfare leads to dependency<br>> Free market<br>> It is more evil than necessary | > Accepts the state being active in society<br>> Accepts welfare<br>> Willing to accept a mixed economy<br>> It is more necessary than evil |
| Rationalism       | Egoistical rationalism                                                                                                    | Altruistic rationalism                                                                                                                      |
| Equality          | Believe individuals are born into a society with equality of opportunity                                                  | Believe the state should play a role in creating equality of opportunity                                                                    |
| Liberal democracy | Suspicious of growing democracy                                                                                           | Values the protective benefits of democracy                                                                                                 |
